 Dharmendra Yadav will be the party candidate from Badayun, Akshay Yadav from Firozabad, Kamlesh Katheria Etawah, Bhailal Cole Robertsganj and Shabbir Balmiki from Bahraich
 suchi par sapa ke rashtriya mahasachiv ram gopal yadav ke dastakhat hai
 The party has left the Mainpuri seat for Mulayam, who is currently an MP from Azamgarh
 vah 1996, 2004 or 2009 main mainpuri kaa pratinidhitiv loksabhaa main kar chuke hai
 Mulayam contested the 2014 elections from Azamgarh and Mainpuri and won both places
 kannauj se maujuuda saansad dimpal yadav ko phir se isi seat se ummidavaar banaaya gaya he

 ) Inbox By Google band hone vaala he
 The company had already announced its closure, but its date was not told then
 ab logon ko notification ke jariye bataaya ja rahaa he
 From April 2, Google will discontinue its Inbox By Google service
 google ne haal hi main apane chat ap Allo ko bhi shatdown kar diya he
 Google launched Inbox by Google in 2014 and will be discontinued on 2 April
 aapako bataa den ki 2 april ko hi google apana soshal network Google Plus bhi band karegi
 In the notifications being sent to users, it has been said, 'this app will be going away in 13 days'
 yahaan yah bhi kaha gaya he ki aapke fevorett inbox feechar ab jimail ap main mil rahe hai
 The logic is that when the company started Inbox by Google, it had many advanced features
 lekin dhire dhire company ne is ap ke fitures standard jimail ap main dene shuru kiye or kuch fitures web main bhi die jane lage
 Therefore, there is no significant value of this app and perhaps this is the reason that Google is preparing to close it completely
 kuch maheene pehle se google ne kuch bache hue nae fitures jo shuruyaat main inbox main the use bhi ab jimail ke standard ap main de rahi he
 However, there are many such features which are still in this app of Google named Inbox and Google has not given them in standard Gmail app till now

 kisi mobile number yaa sim se riyayati dar par ab ek din main keval 100 esemes hi kiye ja sakenge
 Telecom regulator TRAI has taken this initiative as part of its efforts to control unwanted SMS
 niamak ne kaha he ki 100 esemes kii seemaa ke baad agar koi esemes bheja jaataa he to us par kam se kam 50 paise prati esemes shulk hoga
 It is noteworthy that despite all efforts of the regulator, customers are continuing to receive SMS from unregistered tele marketing companies
 is tarah kii fermein doorsanchaar companiyon kii riyayati esemes peshkashon kaa phayda uthaati hai
 Telecom Minister Kapil Sibal said last week that he too continues to receive such unsolicited SMS
 unhone kaha, mujhe har do minute main is tarah kaa esemes miltaa he
 TRAI Principal Advisor n Parameswaran told reporters that this step has been taken to prevent misuse of concessional s MS schemes by non-registered telemarketing companies 
 tippaniyan He said, implementation of these changes and orders will be done in 15 days
 unhone kaha ki is disha main yah pahal he jabaki or kadam uthaae jaaenge
 Telecom operators have also been asked to resolve this within three months and create a system in which, to ensure that no more than 200 smss can be sent with a single signature in an hour
 graahak bhi emsam ke jariye hi avaanchit vyavsaayik sandeshon ke khilaaf shikaayat kar sakate hai
 Parameswaran said that this complaint can be made through SMS on 1909 number
 isamen esemes milane kii tithi or uskaa number bhi saath hona chahie
 The regulator has said that if an SMS is sent after the 100 SMS limit, it will be charged at least 50 paise per SMS
 ullekhneey he ki niamak ke tamaam prayaason ke baavjood graahakon ko gaiyr panjikrut tele marketing companiyon se esemes aane kaa silsilaa jari he

 1
 Honesty is a very important habit
 This is the first habit that you should tell your child about
 koshish kiijie ki paanch saal kaa hone se pehle hi eemaandaaree uske vyavhaar main aa jaae

 It has been asked how much information should be given to the media about the accused and the crime before the FIR is registered? To what extent can the media be informed about the accused after the FIR is registered? Can the accused be given his photo or video when arrested? Can a parade be held in front of the media? Can the identity of the victim be given? Can the details related to the investigation of a case be shared with the media? To what extent? To what extent should the media be informed about the incident if there is a possibility of inciting community violence? How should such information be given to the media so that the perpetrator is alerted to avoid the police? In the sexual offenses with women, the details of the victim and any kind of identification should be given to the media? Cases involving minors What should be done with them?  ) west indies cricket team ko ek karaara jhatka dete hue antarrashtriya cricket parishad (isisi) ne uske of-spin gendbaaj shen shillingford ko sandigdh gendbaaji ection ke aarope main nilambit kar diya he, jabaki unke ek anya gendbaaj marlon sampuls kii tej genden bhi niyamon ke anuroop nahin pai gayi
 "an independent biochemical analysis has found the bowling action of West Indies off-spinner Shane Shillingford to be questionable and in this condition the player has been suspended from bowling in international cricket," the ICC said in a statement
 
 
 '' The assessment reveals that Shane Shillingford's elbows in both, off-break and 'second' balls' action are bent over a maximum of 15 degrees according to ICC rules
 isisi ke anusaar, ''use (shen shillingford ko) tab tak antarrashtriya cricket main gendbaaji se nilambit kar diya gaya he, jab tak vah dobaaraa vishleshan nahin kar letaa, jisase pataa chalegaa ki usne apane gendbaaji ection main sudhaar kiya he
 
 
 '' is bich marlon sampuls ke gendbaaji ection ke swatantra akalan main unki of-brake gend sahi thi, lekin tej gend main uski kohni 15 degree se adhik mud rahi he, jo sandigdh maani jaati he, isliye marlon sampuls ko antarrashtriya cricket main of-brake genden phenkane kii anumati he, lekin unhen tej gend phenkane se roak diya gaya he
 "if Samuels is reported again for suspected bowling action in the next two years, such a report would be considered as the second report in the ICC Rules," the ICC said
 
 
 '' The International Cricket Council said, "marlon Samuels' bowling action is questionable after independent biochemical analysis of the second report, whether it is for a fast ball or for any other type of ball, then he is automatically at least Will be suspended from bowling in international cricket for 12 months
 
 
 '' The bowling of Shane Shillingford and Marlon Samuels was reported by on-field umpires Richard Kettleborough and Nigel Long, TV umpire Vineet Kulkarni and match referee Andy Pycroft at the end of the second day of the Mumbai Test against India last month

 majlis-e-ittehadul Muslimeen (MIM), which is supporting the Congress government of Andhra Pradesh from outside, announced the withdrawal of support to Chief Minister N
 kiran kumaar reddy ke netritv vaali congress sarkaar kii peshaani par bal laa diya he
 The government is already craving for a substantial majority
 centre main bhi alpamat hone kaa dansh jhel rahe sanyukt pragatisheel gathbandhan (samprag) ko emm ne jhatka diya
 In the executive meeting held here, majlis-e-ittehadul Muslimeen (MIM) announced the withdrawal of support from the central and Andhra Pradesh government
 294 sadasyeey andhra vidhansabha main sattadhari party ke sadasyon kii sankhya 155 thi, lekin teen vidhayakon ne baad main wiesar congress party kaa daaman tham liya
 The number of Congress mlas now stands at 152, which is just four more than the 148 required for a simple majority
 kuch or vidhayakon ke wiesar congress main jane kii sambhaavna he
 If opposition parties bring a no-confidence motion and disgruntled mlas cross-voting, the government may be in deep trouble
 mukhya vipakshi telugu desham party (tedepa) ke 86 vidhayak hai, wiesar congress party or telugana raashtra samiti ke 17-17, bhartiya communist party (bhakpa) ke chaar, bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ke teen, marxvaadi communist party (makapa) or loksatta ke ek-ek tathaa anya kii sankhya chah he
 a statement issued by the Congress on Monday said that there is no crisis on the government at present
 emm ke pramukh evam party ke ekmaatr saansad asaduddin ovaisi ne party kaaryakarini kii baithak main liye gaye faisle kii yahaan ghoshnaa kii or spasht kiya ki unki party rajya sarkaar kii 'sampradayik' or 'janvirohi' nitiyon ke kaaran ab usase alag rahegi
 Owaisi said in a press conference that his party was forced to take this decision because Kiran Kumar Reddy's government in Andhra Pradesh displayed communal conduct
 unhone ghoshnaa kii, "ham kiran kumaar reddy kii sarkaar kaa ghatak nahin rahenge
 In such a situation, it is not appropriate that i continue to support the UPA
 ham samprag sarkaar se bhi samarthan waapas lenge
 " aawaisi ne raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ko fax bhejkar unhen party ke faisle se avgat karaayaa or unase milane kaa samay maanga
 He wants to meet in person and tell them under what circumstances the party has taken this decision
 hyderabad se saansad ovaisi ne kaha ki unki party faisla lene ke baad kii raajnneetik paristhatiyon kaa saamana karne ke liye taiyaar he
 He said that his party's mlas would soon meet Governor ESL Narasimha to apprise them of the decision to withdraw support from the Congress government
 rajya or hyderabad main varsh 2010 se ab tak hue sampradayik dangon kaa vistrut byoraa dete hue unhone aarope lagaaya ki congress sarkaar ne na keval emm kii maangon ko nazarandaaj kiya, balki sangh parivaar jaisaa aacharan pradarshit kiya
 MIM took this decision when the government allowed the construction of an umbrella above a temple near the historic Charminar
 party kaa aarope he ki andhra pradesh sarkaar ne adaalat dwaara die gaye yathasthiti behaal rakhane ke aadesh kaa ulanghan kiya he
 Owaisi criticized the Chief Minister for ignoring the High Court order to restore the status quo
 unhone kaha, "congress sarkaar ke is faisle se, uske sampradayik aacharan se, vyarth samay ganvaane se or sangh parivaar ke kaaryakartaaon kaa samarthan karne hyderabad or aasapaas ke ilaakon main nishchit rup se bhaajapa ko majbootee milegi
 These reasons forced us to withdraw support
 " Significantly, MIM has seven mlas in the 295-member assembly
 paryaapt bahumat nahin hone ke kaaran congress sarkaar ke liye emm kaa samarthan mahatvapurn mana ja rahaa he
 When the main opposition Telugu Desam Party (TDP) brought a no-confidence motion last year, MIM saved the government by voting against it
 ovaisi ne yah spasht karte hue ki vah faisle se peeche nahin hatenge, kaha, "is sarkaar kaa patan sunishchit karnaa ab hamaari mukhya praathamikta he
 To highlight the failures of the government, we will go to every corner of the state and ask people how it is issuing anti-people policies and is happy to appease the revolting forces like BJP and Sangh Parivar
 " unhone kaha, "jaganmohan reddy mere mitra hai, kiran kumaar reddy mitra the
 "his remarks indicate that Owaisi's party Jagan's party may ally with the YSR Congress
 is bare main puche jane par unhone kaha ki iskaa jawaab vah chunaav ke samay denge
 The comments emm pramukh ne kaha ki rajya kii maujuuda sarkaar congress ko kamjor kar rahi he
 He said that his party had been supporting the Congress since 1998

 Since the death of Rajasekhara Reddy, several parts of the state and Hyderabad have witnessed communal violence several times
 maujuuda sarkaar kii 'niskriyata' ke kaaran sangh parivaar ke kaaryakartaaon kaa hausala bad gaya he
 The United Progressive Alliance (UPA), which is facing the brunt of being a minority at the center, also slammed the MIM
 yahaan hui kaaryakarini kii baithak main majalis-e-ittehadul muslimin (emm) ne centre or andhra pradesh sarkaar se samarthan waapas lene kii ghoshnaa kar di
 The ruling party had 155 members in the 294-member Andhra Assembly, but the three mlas later joined the YSR Congress Party
 ab congress ke vidhayakon kii sankhya 152 rah gai he jo saamaanya bahumat ke liye vaanchit sankhya 148 se maatr chaar adhik he
 Some more mlas are likely to go to the YSR Congress
 yadi vipakshi dal avishvaas prastaav laate hai or asantusht vidhayak cross voting karte hai to sarkaar gahari musiibat main funs sakati he
 The main opposition Telugu Desam Party (TDP) has 86 mlas, YSR Congress Party and Telangana Rashtra Samithi 17-17, Communist Party of India (CPI), Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP), Marxist Communist Party (CPI) and Loksatta has one each and the number six
 congress kii ore se somvaar ko jari bayaan main kaha gaya he ki sarkaar par philhal koi sankat nahin he
 MIM chief and party's only MP Asaduddin Owaisi announced the decision taken at the party executive meeting here and clarified that his party will now stand apart from it due to the 'communal' and 'anti-people' policies of the state government
 ovaisi ne ek samvaadadaata sammelan main kaha ki unki party yah faisla lene ke liye isliye baadhya hui, kyonki andhra pradesh main kiran kumaar reddy kii sarkaar ne sampradayik aacharan pradarshit kiya
 He declared, "we will no longer be a constituent of Kiran Kumar Reddy's government
 aise main yah uchit nahin he ki main samprag ko samarthan dena jari rakhun
 We will also withdraw support from the UPA government
 " Awaisi sent a fax to President Pranab Mukherjee, apprised him of the party's decision and asked for an appointment
 vah vyaktigat rup se milakar unhen bataanaa chaahate hai ki party ne kin paristhitiyon main yah faisla liya he
 Owaisi, the MP from Hyderabad, said his party was ready to face the political situation after the decision was taken
 unhone kaha ki unki party ke vidhayak congress sarkaar se samarthan waapas liye jane ke faisle se avgat karaane ke liye jald hi rajyapal iesail narsimha se milenge
 Giving a detailed account of the communal riots in the state and Hyderabad since 2010, he alleged that the Congress government not only ignored the demands of MIM but also displayed a Sangh Parivar-like behavior
 emm ne yah faisla tab liya jab sarkaar ne aitihaasik charminar ke sameep sthit ek mandir ke upar chhatari ke nirmaan kii anumati de di
 The party alleges that the Andhra Pradesh government has violated the order given by the court to restore the status quo
 ovaisi ne yathasthiti behaal rakhane ke ucch nyaayalay ke aadesh ko nazarandaaj karne ke liye mukhyamantri kii aalochana kii
 He said, "this decision of the Congress government, its communal conduct, wasted time and support of Sangh Parivar activists will definitely strengthen BJP in Hyderabad and surrounding areas
" inhen vajahon ne hamen samarthan waapas lene ke liye baadhya kiya
 " gauratlab he ki 295 sadasyeey vidhansabha main emm ke saat vidhayak hai
 The support of MIM is considered important for the Congress government due to not having a sufficient majority
 pichley varsh mukhya vipakshi telugu desham party (tedepa) ne jab avishvaas prastaav laayaa tha, tab emm ne hi virodh main matdaan kar sarkaar ko bachaaya tha
 Owaisi, clarifying that he would not back down from the verdict, said, "ensuring the downfall of this government is now our main priority

 unhone kaha, "congress sarkaar ke is faisle se, uske sampradayik aacharan se, vyarth samay ganvaane se or sangh parivaar ke kaaryakartaaon kaa samarthan karne hyderabad or aasapaas ke ilaakon main nishchit rup se bhaajapa ko majbootee milegi
 These reasons forced us to withdraw support
 " Significantly, MIM has seven mlas in the 295-member assembly
 paryaapt bahumat nahin hone ke kaaran congress sarkaar ke liye emm kaa samarthan mahatvapurn mana ja rahaa he

 ovaisi ne yah spasht karte hue ki vah faisle se peeche nahin hatenge, kaha, "is sarkaar kaa patan sunishchit karnaa ab hamaari mukhya praathamikta he

 a statement issued by the Congress on Monday said that there is no crisis on the government at present
 emm ke pramukh evam party ke ekmaatr saansad asaduddin ovaisi ne party kaaryakarini kii baithak main liye gaye faisle kii yahaan ghoshnaa kii or spasht kiya ki unki party rajya sarkaar kii 'sampradayik' or 'janvirohi' nitiyon ke kaaran ab usase alag rahegi
 Owaisi said in a press conference that his party was forced to take this decision because Kiran Kumar Reddy's government in Andhra Pradesh displayed communal conduct
 unhone ghoshnaa kii, "ham kiran kumaar reddy kii sarkaar kaa ghatak nahin rahenge
 In such a situation, it is not appropriate that i continue to support the UPA
 ham samprag sarkaar se bhi samarthan waapas lenge
 " aawaisi ne raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ko fax bhejkar unhen party ke faisle se avgat karaayaa or unase milane kaa samay maanga
 He wants to meet in person and tell them under what circumstances the party has taken this decision
 hyderabad se saansad ovaisi ne kaha ki unki party faisla lene ke baad kii raajnneetik paristhatiyon kaa saamana karne ke liye taiyaar he
 He said that his party's mlas would soon meet Governor ESL Narasimha to apprise them of the decision to withdraw support from the Congress government
 rajya or hyderabad main varsh 2010 se ab tak hue sampradayik dangon kaa vistrut byoraa dete hue unhone aarope lagaaya ki congress sarkaar ne na keval emm kii maangon ko nazarandaaj kiya, balki sangh parivaar jaisaa aacharan pradarshit kiya

 Since the death of Rajasekhara Reddy, several parts of the state and Hyderabad have witnessed communal violence several times
 maujuuda sarkaar kii 'niskriyata' ke kaaran sangh parivaar ke kaaryakartaaon kaa hausala bad gaya he
 MIM chief and party's only MP Asaduddin Owaisi announced the decision taken at the party executive meeting here and clarified that his party will now stand apart from it due to the 'communal' and 'anti-people' policies of the state government
 ovaisi ne ek samvaadadaata sammelan main kaha ki unki party yah faisla lene ke liye isliye baadhya hui, kyonki andhra pradesh main kiran kumaar reddy kii sarkaar ne sampradayik aacharan pradarshit kiya
 He declared, "we will no longer be a constituent of Kiran Kumar Reddy's government
 aise main yah uchit nahin he ki main samprag ko samarthan dena jari rakhun
 We will also withdraw support from the UPA government
 " Awaisi sent a fax to President Pranab Mukherjee, apprised him of the party's decision and asked for an appointment
 vah vyaktigat rup se milakar unhen bataanaa chaahate hai ki party ne kin paristhitiyon main yah faisla liya he
 Owaisi, the MP from Hyderabad, said his party was ready to face the political situation after the decision was taken
 unhone kaha ki unki party ke vidhayak congress sarkaar se samarthan waapas liye jane ke faisle se avgat karaane ke liye jald hi rajyapal iesail narsimha se milenge
 Giving a detailed account of the communal riots in the state and Hyderabad since 2010, he alleged that the Congress government not only ignored the demands of MIM but also displayed a Sangh Parivar-like behavior
 emm ne yah faisla tab liya jab sarkaar ne aitihaasik charminar ke sameep sthit ek mandir ke upar chhatari ke nirmaan kii anumati de di
 The party alleges that the Andhra Pradesh government has violated the order given by the court to restore the status quo
 ovaisi ne yathasthiti behaal rakhane ke ucch nyaayalay ke aadesh ko nazarandaaj karne ke liye mukhyamantri kii aalochana kii
 He said, "this decision of the Congress government, its communal conduct, wasted time and support of Sangh Parivar activists will definitely strengthen BJP in Hyderabad and surrounding areas
" inhen vajahon ne hamen samarthan waapas lene ke liye baadhya kiya
 " gauratlab he ki 295 sadasyeey vidhansabha main emm ke saat vidhayak hai
 The support of MIM is considered important for the Congress government due to not having a sufficient majority
 pichley varsh mukhya vipakshi telugu desham party (tedepa) ne jab avishvaas prastaav laayaa tha, tab emm ne hi virodh main matdaan kar sarkaar ko bachaaya tha
 Owaisi, clarifying that he would not back down from the verdict, said, "ensuring the downfall of this government is now our main priority
 sarkaar kii naakaamiyon ko ujagar karne ke liye ham rajya ke kone-kone main jaaenge or logon se kahenge ki yah kis tarah janvirohi nitiyaan jari kar rahi he tathaa bhaajapa va sangh parivaar jaisi phirakaaprast takaton ko khush karne main lagi hui he
 "he said," Jaganmohan Reddy is my friend, Kiran Kumar Reddy was a friend
 " unki is tippanee se yah sanket mil rahaa he ki ovaisi kii party jagan kii party wiesar congress ke saath gathbandhan kar sakati he
 When asked about this, he said that he will answer this at the time of election

 vahaan ke khalipha ko muslim ke dharmik pradhan ke rup main dekha jaataa tha

 vahiin, is dauraan rashtrapita mahatma gandhi ke netritv main 1 agast 1920 ko angrejon ke khilaaf pehla jan andolan shuru hua
